My criteria for buying great perfumes is a little less discriminating (on some counts): 1) I can afford it, 2) it's different from what I already own, and 3) it doesn't give me a headache. For me, that makes Lovely an exceptional fragrance. I find Lovely to be a beautiful, complex, slightly unisex perfume with floral and woody accords. There are some fruity notes listed that don't quite come out on my skin, so the whole scent smells dry rather than sweet on me, which is definitely a plus: sweet perfumes intesify on my skin and lead to headaches and sneezing.<br /><br />The sillage for Lovely stays quite close (another thing I look for in perfumes, but I realize others may not). This gives it an intimate feel in my mind, making it cozy and feminine. It's office-friendly, but also date-worthy, depending on what your date likes (my fiance loves this perfume on me).<br /><br />If you're looking for a budget-friendly perfume that doesn't smell budget-friendly, I highly recommend checking out Lovely.
